_getHealthColor(health) {\n362\t        // Interpolate from red (0) through yellow (0.5) to green (1)\n363\t        var r, g, b;\n364\t        if (health < 0.5) {\n365\t            // Red to yellow\n366\t            var t = health * 2; // 0-0.5 maps to 0-1\n367\t            r = 0.94; // 0xef/255\n368\t            g = 0.31 + t * 0.61; // 0x4f → 0xeab3 (approx)\n369\t            b = 0.14 +   _scene.add(ceil);\n        _roomObjs.ceiling = ceil;\n\n        // walls (semi-transparent, double-sided)\n        const wallMat = new THREE.MeshLambertMaterial({ color: 0x243040, transparent: true, opacity: 0.13, side: THREE.DoubleSide });\n        [\n            { pw: w, ry: 0,           px: cx,    py: h / 2, pz: oz     },\n            { pw: w, ry: Math.PI,     px: cx,    py: h / 2, pz: oz + d * Apply floor plan calibration to the ground plane texture.\n     * @param {Object} calibration - Calibration data from API\n     * @param {number} calibration.meters_per_pixel - Scale factor\n     * @param {number} calibration.rotation_deg - Rotation angle in degrees\n     * @param {number} calibration.cal_ax - Point A X coordinate\n     * @param {number} calibration.cal_ay - Point A Y coordinate\n     * @param {number} calibration.cal_bx - Point B X coordinate\n     * @param {number} calibration.cal_by - Point B Y coordinate\n     * @param {number} calibration.distance_m - Real-world distance in meters\n     */\n    function setFloorPlanCalibration(calibration) {\n        if (!calibration) return;\n\n        _floorCalibration = {\n            metersPerPixel: calibration.meters_per_pixel || 1,\n            rotationDeg: calibration.rotation_deg || 0,\n            ax: calibration.cal_ax || 0,\n            ay: calibration.cal_ay || 0,\n            bx: calibration.cal_bx || 0,\n            by: calibration.cal_by || 0,\n            distanceM: calibration.distance_m || 1\n        };\n\n        // Apply calibration to floor texture if floor exists\n        if (_roomObjs.floor && _floorTex) {\n            _applyCalibrationToFloor();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Apply stored calibration to the floor mesh.\n     * Uses texture transformation matrix to scale and rotate.\n     */\n    function _applyCalibrationToFloor() {\n        if (!_roomObjs.floor || !_floorTex) return;\n\n        const floor = _roomObjs.floor;\n        const tex = _floorTex;\n\n        // Enable texture transformation\n        tex.matrixAutoUpdate = false;\n\n        // Calculate texture scale based on room dimensions vs image dimensions\n        // Default room size if not set\n        const roomWidth = _room ? _room.width : 10;\n        const roomDepth = _room ? _room.depth : 10;\n\n        // Calculate how many meters the image covers at current scale\n        const imageWidthMeters = tex.image.width * _floorCalibration.metersPerPixel;\n        const imageHeightMeters = tex.image.height * _floorCalibration.metersPerPixel;\n\n        // Scale texture to fit room\n        const scaleX = roomWidth / imageWidthMeters;\n        const scaleY = roomDepth / imageHeightMeters;\n\n        // Build transformation matrix: center -> rotate -> scale -> center back\n        tex.matrix.setUvTransform(\n            0.5, 0.5,           // center\n            scaleX, scaleY,     // scale\n            _floorCalibration.rotationDeg * Math.PI / 180,  // rotation\n            0, 0                // translation\n        );\n\n        floor.material.needsUpdate = true;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get current floor plan calibration state.\n     * @returns {Object} Current calibration data\n     */\n    function getFloorPlanCalibration() {\n        return _floorCalibration;\n    }\n\n    // ── node meshes => {\n            if (!incoming.has(mac)) { _scene.remove(m); _nodeMeshes.delete(mac); }\n        });\n        nodes.forEach(n => {\n            let m = _nodeMeshes.get(n.mac);\n            if (!m)     */\n    function _createRouterMesh() {\n        const routerGroup = new THREE.Group();\n\n        // Router body (horizontal box)\n        const bodyGeo = new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.16, 0.04, 0.1);\n link based on health score.\n     * Green (#22c55e at health=1.0) → Yellow (#eab308 at health=0.5) → Red (#ef4444 at health=0)\n     * @param {number} health - Health score in [0, 1]\n     * @returns {number} Three.js color hex value\n     */\n    function _getHealthColor(health) {\n        // Interpolate from red (0) through yellow (0.5) to green (1)\n        var r, g, b;\n        if (health < 0.5) {\n            // Red to yellow\n            var t = health * 2; // 0-0.5 maps to 0-1\n            r = 0.94; // 0xef/255\n            g = 0.31 + t * 0.61; // 0x4f → 0xeab3 (approx)\n            b = 0.14 + t * 0.06;\n        } else {\n            // Yellow to green\n            var t = (health - 0.5) * 2; // 0.5-1 maps to 0-1\n            r = 0.92 - t * 0.78; // 0xeab3 → 0x22\n            g = 0.69 + t * 0.09; // stays mostly yellow-green\n            b = 0.08 + t * 0.28; // 0x08 → 0x5e\n        }\n        return (Math.round(r * 255) << 16) | (Math.round(g * 255) << 8) | Math.round(b * 255);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get link line thickness based on health score.\n     * health > 0.7 → 2px, health 0.4-0.7 → 1px, health < 0.4 → 0.5px\n     * @param {number} health - Health score in [0, 1]\n     * @returns {number} Line thickness\n     */\n    function _getHealthThickness(health) {\n        if (health > 0.7) return 2;\n        if (health >= 0.4) return 1;\n        return 0.5;\n healthScore * 0.5;\n\n            const geo = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([a.position.clone(), b.position.clone()]);\n            const line = new THREE.Line(geo, new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({\n                color: healthColor,\n                transparent: true,\n                opacity: opacity,\n                linewidth: thickness // Note: linewidth > 1 only Link distance d = |P1 - P2|\n68\t     * - WiFi wavelength lambda: 5 GHz -> lambda = 0.06m, 2.4 GHz -> lambda = 0.125m\n69\t     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n70\t     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - Link distance d = |P1 - P2|\n     * - WiFi wavelength lambda: 5 GHz -> lambda = 0.06m, 2.4 GHz -> lambda = 0.125m\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     * - Ellipsoid centre: midpoint(P1, P2)\n     * - Ellipsoid orientation: major axis along the P1->P2 unit vector\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel) {\n        // Get wavelength based on channel\n        const lambda = getWavelengthForChannel(channel);\n\n        // Direct distance between TX and RX\n        const d = tx.distanceTo(rx);\n\n        // First Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters\n        // Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n        const a = (d + lambda / 2) / 2;\n\n        // Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @param {number} zoneNumber - Fresnel zone number (1-based, typically 1-5)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b, zoneNumber }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, zoneNumber) {\n        // Get wavelength based on channel\n        const lambda = getWavelengthForChannel(channel);\n\n        // Direct distance between TX and RX\n        const d = tx.distanceTo(rx);\n\n        // nth Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters\n        // Semi-major axis: a = (d + n*lambda/2) / 2\n        const n = Math.max(1, zoneNumber);\n        const a = (d + n * lambda / 2) / 2;\n\n        // Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n        // Using the property that for a prolate spheroid with foci at tx and rx:\n        // b^2 = a^2 - (d/2)^2\n        const b = Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, a * a - (d / 2) * (d / 2)));\n\n        // Center of ellipsoid (midpoint between TX and RX)\n        const center = new THREE.Vector3().addVectors(tx, rx).multiplyScalar(0.5);\n\n        // Rotation: align with TX-RX axis\n        // X-axis is the major axis of the ellipsoid (a), Y and Z are minor (b)\n        const direction = new THREE.Vector3().subVectors(rx, tx).normalize();\n        const xAxis = new THREE.Vector3(1, 0, 0);\n        const quaternion = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(xAxis, direction);\n\n        return {\n            center: center,\n            semiAxes: new THREE.Vector3(a, b, b), // X (major along link), Y, Z (minor)\n            rotation: quaternion,\n            lambda: lambda,\n            d: d,\n            a: a,\n            b: b,\n            zoneNumber: n,\n            channel: channel\n        };\n    }","originalFile":"/**\n * Spaxel Dashboard - Fresnel Zone Helper Module\n *\n * Shared Fresnel zone ellipsoid geometry computation for:\n * - Debug overlay (all active links)\n * - Explainability overlay (contributing links for a specific blob)\n *\n * Provides FresnelEllipsoid() function that returns Three.js meshes\n * ready for scene insertion.\n */\n\n(function() {\n    'use strict';\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Configuration\n    // ============================================\n    const CONFIG = {\n        // WiFi wavelengths (c/f in meters)\n        wavelength_5ghz: 0.06,      // 5 GHz\n        wavelength_2_4ghz: 0.125,   // 2.4 GHz\n        // Geometry\n        sphereSegments: 32,         // Sphere geometry segments (reduced on mobile)\n        sphereHeightSegments: 16,\n        wireframeOpacity: 0.6,      // Line opacity for wireframe\n        fillOpacity: 0.08,          // Fill opacity\n        mobileViewportWidth: 768,    // Width threshold for mobile\n        mobileSegments: 16,         // Reduced segments for mobile\n        mobileHeightSegments: 8\n    };\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Private State\n    // ============================================\n    let _scene = null;\n\n    /**\n     * Initialize the Fresnel module with the Three.js scene.\n     * @param {THREE.Scene} scene - (d/2)^2)\n     * - Ellipsoid centre: midpoint(P1, P2)\n     * - Ellipsoid orientation: major axis along the P1->P2 unit vector\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel) {\n        // Get wavelength based on channel\n        const lambda = getWavelengthForChannel(channel);\n\n        // Direct distance between TX and RX\n        const d = tx.distanceTo(rx);\n\n        // First Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters\n        // Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n        const a = (d + lambda / 2) / 2;\n\n        // Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - Call Fresnel.init(scene) first.');\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        options = options || {};\n        const wireframeOpacity = options.wireframeOpacity !== undefined ? options.wireframeOpacity : CONFIG.wireframeOpacity;\n        const fillOpacity = options.fillOpacity !== undefined ? options.fillOpacity : CONFIG.fillOpacity;\n\n        // Calculate ellipsoid geometry\n        const ellipsoid = calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel);\n\n        // Determine segment count based on viewport (mobile optimization)\n        const isMobile = window.innerWidth < CONFIG.mobileViewportWidth;\n        const segments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileSegments : CONFIG.sphereSegments;\n        const heightSegments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileHeightSegments : CONFIG.sphereHeightSegments;\n\n        // Create unit sphere geometry — will be scaled via mesh.scale\n        const geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(1, segments, heightSegments);\n\n        // Create wireframe using EdgesGeometry for crisp edges\n        const edgesGeometry = new THREE.EdgesGeometry(geometry);\n        const wireframeMaterial = new color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: fillOpacity,\n            depthWrite: false,\n            side: THREE.DoubleSide\n        });\n        const fill = new fill.scale.copy(ellipsoid.semiAxes);\n\n        // Position at ellipsoid center\n        wireframe.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n        fill.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n\n        // Apply from addFresnelEllipsoid or FresnelEllipsoid\n     */\n    function removeFresnelEllipsoid(ellipsoid) {\n        if (!ellipsoid) return;\n\n        if (ellipsoid.wireframe) {\n            if (_scene) Call Fresnel.init(scene) first.');\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        options = options || {};\n        const wireframeOpacity = options.wireframeOpacity !== undefined ? options.wireframeOpacity : CONFIG.wireframeOpacity;\n        const fillOpacity = options.fillOpacity !== undefined ? options.fillOpacity : CONFIG.fillOpacity;\n        const zoneNumber = options.zoneNumber || 1;\n\n        // Calculate ellipsoid geometry for the specified zone\n        const ellipsoid = calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, zoneNumber);","originalFile":"/**\n * Spaxel Dashboard - Fresnel Zone Helper Module\n *\n * Shared Fresnel zone ellipsoid geometry computation for:\n * - Debug overlay (all active links)\n * - Explainability overlay (contributing links for a specific blob)\n *\n * Provides FresnelEllipsoid() function that returns Three.js meshes\n * ready for scene insertion.\n */\n\n(function() {\n    'use strict';\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Configuration\n    // ============================================\n    const CONFIG = {\n        // WiFi wavelengths (c/f in meters)\n        wavelength_5ghz: 0.06,      // 5 GHz\n        wavelength_2_4ghz: 0.125,   // 2.4 GHz\n        // Geometry\n        sphereSegments: 32,         // Sphere geometry segments (reduced on mobile)\n        sphereHeightSegments: 16,\n        wireframeOpacity: 0.6,      // Line opacity for wireframe\n        fillOpacity: 0.08,          // Fill opacity\n        mobileViewportWidth: 768,    // Width threshold for mobile\n        mobileSegments: 16,         // Reduced segments for mobile\n        mobileHeightSegments: 8\n    };\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Private State\n    // ============================================\n    let _scene = null;\n\n    /**\n     * Initialize the Fresnel module with the Three.js scene.\n     * @param {THREE.Scene} scene - The Three.js scene\n     */\n    function init(scene) {\n        _scene = scene;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get WiFi wavelength based on channel number.\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel (1-14 for 2.4 GHz, 36-165 for 5 GHz)\n     * @returns {number} Wavelength in meters\n     */\n    function getWavelengthForChannel(channel) {\n        if (!channel || channel < 1) return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n\n        // 2.4 GHz channels: 1-14\n        if (channel <= 14) {\n            return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n        }\n\n        // 5 GHz channels: 36 and above\n        return CONFIG.wavelength_5ghz;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Calculate Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters for a link.\n     * Based on the first Fresnel zone geometry.\n     *\n     * For a link with TX at position P1 and RX at position P2:\n     * - Link distance d = |P1 - P2|\n     * - WiFi wavelength lambda: 5 GHz -> lambda = 0.06m, 2.4 GHz -> lambda = 0.125m\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     * - Ellipsoid centre: midpoint(P1, P2)\n     * - Ellipsoid orientation: major axis along the P1->P2 unit vector\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel) {\n        return calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, 1);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Calculate Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters for a specific zone number.\n     * Based on the nth Fresnel zone geometry.\n     *\n     * For the nth Fresnel zone:\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + n*lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @param {number} zoneNumber - Fresnel zone number (1-based, typically 1-5)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b, zoneNumber }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, zoneNumber) {\n        // Get wavelength based on channel\n        const lambda = getWavelengthForChannel(channel);\n\n        // Direct distance between TX and RX\n        const d = tx.distanceTo(rx);\n\n        // nth Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters\n        // Semi-major axis: a = (d + n*lambda/2) / 2\n        const n = Math.max(1, zoneNumber);\n        const a = (d + n * lambda / 2) / 2;\n\n        // Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n        // Using the property that for a prolate spheroid with foci at tx and rx:\n        // b^2 = a^2 - (d/2)^2\n        const b = Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, a * a - (d / 2) * (d / 2)));\n\n        // Center of ellipsoid (midpoint between TX and RX)\n        const center = new THREE.Vector3().addVectors(tx, rx).multiplyScalar(0.5);\n\n        // Rotation: align with TX-RX axis\n        // X-axis is the major axis of the ellipsoid (a), Y and Z are minor (b)\n        const direction = new THREE.Vector3().subVectors(rx, tx).normalize();\n        const xAxis = new THREE.Vector3(1, 0, 0);\n        const quaternion = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(xAxis, direction);\n\n        return {\n            center: center,\n            semiAxes: new THREE.Vector3(a, b, b), // X (major along link), Y, Z (minor)\n            rotation: quaternion,\n            lambda: lambda,\n            d: d,\n            a: a,\n            b: b,\n            zoneNumber: n,\n            channel: channel\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a Three.js Mesh for a Fresnel zone ellipsoid.\n     * Creates both wireframe and fill meshes for proper visualization.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number\n     * @param {number} color - Color hex value (e.g., 0x4FC3F7 for blue)\n     * @param {Object} options - Optional settings { wireframeOpacity, fillOpacity }\n     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data } meshes\n     */\n    function FresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options) {\n        if (!_scene) {\n            console.warn('[Fresnel] Scene not initialized. Call Fresnel.init(scene) first.');\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        options = options || {};\n        const wireframeOpacity = options.wireframeOpacity !== undefined ? options.wireframeOpacity : CONFIG.wireframeOpacity;\n        const fillOpacity = options.fillOpacity !== undefined ? options.fillOpacity : CONFIG.fillOpacity;\n\n        // Calculate ellipsoid geometry\n        const ellipsoid = calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel);\n\n        // Determine segment count based on viewport (mobile optimization)\n        const isMobile = window.innerWidth < CONFIG.mobileViewportWidth;\n        const segments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileSegments : CONFIG.sphereSegments;\n        const heightSegments = isMobile ? Fresnel Zone Helper Module\n *\n * Shared Fresnel zone ellipsoid geometry computation for:\n * - Debug overlay (all active links)\n * - Explainability overlay (contributing links for a specific blob)\n *\n * Provides FresnelEllipsoid() function that returns Three.js meshes\n * ready for scene insertion.\n */\n\n(function() {\n    'use strict';\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Configuration\n    // ============================================\n    const CONFIG = {\n        // WiFi wavelengths (c/f in meters)\n        wavelength_5ghz: 0.06,      // 5 GHz\n        wavelength_2_4ghz: 0.125,   // 2.4 GHz\n        // Geometry\n        sphereSegments: 32,         // Sphere geometry segments (reduced on mobile)\n        sphereHeightSegments: 16,\n        wireframeOpacity: 0.6,      // Line opacity for wireframe\n        fillOpacity: 0.08,          // Fill opacity\n        mobileViewportWidth: 768,    // Width threshold for mobile\n        mobileSegments: 16,         // Reduced segments for mobile\n        mobileHeightSegments: 8\n    };\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Private State\n    // ============================================\n    let _scene = null;\n\n    /**\n     * Initialize the Fresnel module with the Three.js scene.\n     * @param {THREE.Scene} scene - Link distance d = |P1 - P2|\n     * - WiFi wavelength lambda: 5 GHz -> lambda = 0.06m, 2.4 GHz -> lambda = 0.125m\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     * - Ellipsoid centre: midpoint(P1, P2)\n     * - Ellipsoid orientation: major axis along the P1->P2 unit vector\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel) {\n        return calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, 1);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Calculate Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters for a specific zone number.\n     * Based on the nth Fresnel zone geometry.\n     *\n     * For the nth Fresnel zone:\n     * - (d/2)^2)\n        // Using the property that for a prolate spheroid with foci at tx and rx:\n        // b^2 = a^2 - (d/2)^2\n        const b = Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, a * a - (d / 2) * (d / 2)));\n\n        // Center of ellipsoid (midpoint between TX and RX)\n        const center = new THREE.Vector3().addVectors(tx, rx).multiplyScalar(0.5);\n\n        // Rotation: align with TX-RX axis\n        // X-axis is the major axis of the ellipsoid (a), Y and Z are minor (b)\n        const direction = new THREE.Vector3().subVectors(rx, tx).normalize();\n        const xAxis = new THREE.Vector3(1, 0, 0);\n        const quaternion = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(xAxis, direction);\n\n        return {\n            center: center,\n            semiAxes: new THREE.Vector3(a, b, b), // X (major along link), Y, Z (minor)\n            rotation: quaternion,\n            lambda: lambda,\n            d: d,\n            a: a,\n            b: b,\n            zoneNumber: n,\n            channel: channel\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a Three.js Mesh for a Fresnel zone ellipsoid.\n     * Creates both wireframe and fill meshes for proper visualization.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Optional settings { wireframeOpacity, fillOpacity, zoneNumber }\n     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data } meshes\n     */\n    function FresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options) {\n        if (!_scene) {\n            console.warn('[Fresnel] Scene not initialized. Call Fresnel.init(scene) first.');\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        options = options || {};\n        const wireframeOpacity = options.wireframeOpacity !== undefined ? options.wireframeOpacity : CONFIG.wireframeOpacity;\n        const fillOpacity = options.fillOpacity !== undefined ? options.fillOpacity : CONFIG.fillOpacity;\n        const zoneNumber = options.zoneNumber || 1;\n\n        // Calculate ellipsoid geometry for the specified zone\n        const ellipsoid = calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, zoneNumber);\n\n        // Determine segment count based on viewport (mobile optimization)\n        const isMobile = window.innerWidth < CONFIG.mobileViewportWidth;\n        const segments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileSegments : CONFIG.sphereSegments;\n        const heightSegments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileHeightSegments : CONFIG.sphereHeightSegments;\n\n        // Create unit sphere geometry — will be scaled via mesh.scale\n        const geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(1, segments, heightSegments);\n\n        // Create wireframe using EdgesGeometry for crisp edges\n        const edgesGeometry = new THREE.EdgesGeometry(geometry);\n        const wireframeMaterial = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({\n            color: color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: wireframeOpacity,\n            depthTest: true,\n            depthWrite: false\n        });\n        const wireframe = new THREE.LineSegments(edgesGeometry, wireframeMaterial);\n\n        // Create fill mesh\n        const fillMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({\n            color: color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: fillOpacity,\n            depthWrite: false,\n            side: THREE.DoubleSide\n        });\n        const fill = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, fillMaterial);\n\n        // Apply non-uniform scaling: X = semi-major (a), Y = semi-minor (b), Z = semi-minor (b)\n        wireframe.scale.copy(ellipsoid.semiAxes);\n        fill.scale.copy(ellipsoid.semiAxes);\n\n        // Position at ellipsoid center\n        wireframe.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n        fill.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n\n        // Apply rotation to align with link axis\n        wireframe.quaternion.copy(ellipsoid.rotation);\n        fill.quaternion.copy(ellipsoid.rotation);\n\n        // Store metadata for raycasting and interactions\n        const data = {\n            tx: tx.clone(),\n            rx: rx.clone(),\n            channel: channel,\n            lambda: ellipsoid.lambda,\n            d: ellipsoid.d,\n            a: ellipsoid.a,\n            b: ellipsoid.b,\n            semiAxes: ellipsoid.semiAxes.clone(),\n            center: ellipsoid.center.clone(),\n            rotation: ellipsoid.rotation.clone()\n        };\n\n        wireframe.userData = { fresnelEllipsoid: data };\n        fill.userData = { fresnelEllipsoid: data };\n\n        return {\n            wireframe: wireframe,\n            fill: fill,\n            data: data\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a Fresnel ellipsoid to the scene.\n     * Convenience function that creates and adds the mesh.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number\n     * @param {number} color - Color hex value\n     * @param {Object} options - Optional settings\n     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data }\n     */\n    function addFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options) {\n from addFresnelEllipsoid or FresnelEllipsoid\n     */\n    function removeFresnelEllipsoid(ellipsoid) {\n        if (!ellipsoid) return;\n\n        if (ellipsoid.wireframe) {\n            if (_scene) ellipsoid.fill.geometry.dispose();\n            if (ellipsoid.fill.material) ellipsoid.fill.material.dispose();\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Public Fresnel Zone Helper Module\n *\n * Shared Fresnel zone ellipsoid geometry computation for:\n * - Debug overlay (all active links)\n * - Explainability overlay (contributing links for a specific blob)\n *\n * Provides FresnelEllipsoid() function that returns Three.js meshes\n * ready for scene insertion.\n */\n\n(function() {\n    'use strict';\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Configuration\n    // ============================================\n    const CONFIG = {\n        // WiFi wavelengths (c/f in meters)\n        wavelength_5ghz: 0.06,      // 5 GHz\n        wavelength_2_4ghz: 0.125,   // 2.4 GHz\n        // Geometry\n        sphereSegments: 32,         // Sphere geometry segments (reduced on mobile)\n        sphereHeightSegments: 16,\n        wireframeOpacity: 0.6,      // Line opacity for wireframe\n        fillOpacity: 0.08,          // Fill opacity\n        mobileViewportWidth: 768,    // Width threshold for mobile\n        mobileSegments: 16,         // Reduced segments for mobile\n        mobileHeightSegments: 8\n    };\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Private State\n    // ============================================\n    let _scene = null;\n\n    /**\n     * Initialize the Fresnel module with the Three.js scene.\n     * @param {THREE.Scene} scene - The Three.js scene\n     */\n    function init(scene) {\n        _scene = scene;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get WiFi wavelength based on channel number.\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel (1-14 for 2.4 GHz, 36-165 for 5 GHz)\n     * @returns {number} Wavelength in meters\n     */\n    function getWavelengthForChannel(channel) {\n        if (!channel || channel < 1) return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n\n        // 2.4 GHz channels: 1-14\n        if (channel <= 14) {\n            return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n        }\n\n        // 5 GHz channels: 36 and above\n        return CONFIG.wavelength_5ghz;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Calculate Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters for a link.\n     * Based on the first Fresnel zone geometry.\n     *\n     * For a link with TX at position P1 and RX at position P2:\n     * - Link distance d = |P1 - P2|\n     * - WiFi wavelength lambda: 5 GHz -> lambda = 0.06m, 2.4 GHz -> lambda = 0.125m\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     * - Ellipsoid centre: midpoint(P1, P2)\n     * - Ellipsoid orientation: major axis along the P1->P2 unit vector\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel) {\n        return calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, 1);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Calculate Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters for a specific zone number.\n     * Based on the nth Fresnel zone geometry.\n     *\n     * For the nth Fresnel zone:\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + n*lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @param {number} zoneNumber - Fresnel zone number (1-based, typically 1-5)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b, zoneNumber }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, zoneNumber) {\n        // Get wavelength based on channel\n        const lambda = getWavelengthForChannel(channel);\n\n        // Direct distance between TX and RX\n        const d = tx.distanceTo(rx);\n\n        // nth Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters\n        // Semi-major axis: a = (d + n*lambda/2) / 2\n        const n = Math.max(1, zoneNumber);\n        const a = (d + n * lambda / 2) / 2;\n\n        // Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n        // Using the property that for a prolate spheroid with foci at tx and rx:\n        // b^2 = a^2 - (d/2)^2\n        const b = Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, a * a - (d / 2) * (d / 2)));\n\n        // Center of ellipsoid (midpoint between TX and RX)\n        const center = new THREE.Vector3().addVectors(tx, rx).multiplyScalar(0.5);\n\n        // Rotation: align with TX-RX axis\n        // X-axis is the major axis of the ellipsoid (a), Y and Z are minor (b)\n        const direction = new THREE.Vector3().subVectors(rx, tx).normalize();\n        const xAxis = new THREE.Vector3(1, 0, 0);\n        const quaternion = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(xAxis, direction);\n\n        return {\n            center: center,\n            semiAxes: new THREE.Vector3(a, b, b), // X (major along link), Y, Z (minor)\n            rotation: quaternion,\n            lambda: lambda,\n            d: d,\n            a: a,\n            b: b,\n            zoneNumber: n,\n            channel: channel\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a Three.js Mesh for a Fresnel zone ellipsoid.\n     * Creates both wireframe and fill meshes for proper visualization.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Call Fresnel.init(scene) first.');\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        options = options || {};\n        const wireframeOpacity = options.wireframeOpacity !== undefined ? options.wireframeOpacity : CONFIG.wireframeOpacity;\n        const fillOpacity = options.fillOpacity !== undefined ? options.fillOpacity : CONFIG.fillOpacity;\n        const zoneNumber = options.zoneNumber || 1;\n\n        // Calculate ellipsoid geometry for the specified zone\n        const ellipsoid = calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, zoneNumber);\n\n        // Determine segment count based on viewport (mobile optimization)\n        const isMobile = window.innerWidth < CONFIG.mobileViewportWidth;\n        const segments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileHeightSegments : CONFIG.sphereHeightSegments;\n\n        // Create unit sphere geometry — will be scaled via mesh.scale\n        const geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(1, segments, heightSegments);\n\n        // Create wireframe using EdgesGeometry for crisp edges\n        const edgesGeometry = new THREE.EdgesGeometry(geometry);\n        const wireframeMaterial = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({\n            color: color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: wireframeOpacity,\n            depthTest: true,\n            depthWrite: false\n        });\n color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: fillOpacity,\n            depthWrite: false,\n            side: THREE.DoubleSide\n        });\n        const fill = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, fillMaterial);\n\n        // Apply non-uniform scaling: X = semi-major (a), Y = semi-minor (b), Z = semi-minor (b)\n        wireframe.scale.copy(ellipsoid.semiAxes);\n        fill.scale.copy(ellipsoid.semiAxes);\n\n        // Position at ellipsoid center\n        wireframe.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n        fill.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n\n        // Apply rotation to align with link axis\n        wireframe.quaternion.copy(ellipsoid.rotation);\n        fill.quaternion.copy(ellipsoid.rotation);\n\n        // Store metadata for raycasting and interactions\n        const data = {\n            tx: tx.clone(),\n            rx: rx.clone(),\n            channel: channel,\n            zoneNumber: ellipsoid.zoneNumber,\n            lambda: ellipsoid.lambda,\n            d: ellipsoid.d,\n            a: ellipsoid.a,\n            b: ellipsoid.b,\n            semiAxes: ellipsoid.semiAxes.clone(),\n            center: ellipsoid.center.clone(),\n            rotation: ellipsoid.rotation.clone()\n        };\n\n        wireframe.userData = { fresnelEllipsoid: data };\n        fill.userData = { fresnelEllipsoid: data };\n\n        return {\n            wireframe: wireframe,\n            fill: fill,\n            data: data\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a Fresnel ellipsoid to the scene.\n     * Convenience function that creates and adds the mesh.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number\n     * @param {number} color - Color hex value\n     * @param {Object} options - Optional settings\n     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data }\n     */\n    function addFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options) {\n        const ellipsoid = FresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options);\n        if (!ellipsoid) return null;\n\n        if (_scene) {\n            _scene.add(ellipsoid.wireframe);\n            _scene.add(ellipsoid.fill);\n        }\n\n        return ellipsoid;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Remove a Fresnel ellipsoid Fresnel Zone Helper Module\n *\n * Shared Fresnel zone ellipsoid geometry computation for:\n * - Debug overlay (all active links)\n * - Explainability overlay (contributing links for a specific blob)\n *\n * Provides FresnelEllipsoid() function that returns Three.js meshes\n * ready for scene insertion.\n */\n\n(function() {\n    'use strict';\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Configuration\n    // ============================================\n    const CONFIG = {\n        // WiFi wavelengths (c/f in meters)\n        wavelength_5ghz: 0.06,      // 5 GHz\n        wavelength_2_4ghz: 0.125,   // 2.4 GHz\n        // Geometry\n        sphereSegments: 32,         // Sphere geometry segments (reduced on mobile)\n        sphereHeightSegments: 16,\n        wireframeOpacity: 0.6,      // Line opacity for wireframe\n        fillOpacity: 0.08,          // Fill opacity\n        mobileViewportWidth: 768,    // Width threshold for mobile\n        mobileSegments: 16,         // Reduced segments for mobile\n        mobileHeightSegments: 8\n    };\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Private State\n    // ============================================\n    let _scene = null;\n\n    /**\n     * Initialize the Fresnel module with the Three.js scene.\n     * @param {THREE.Scene} scene - The Three.js scene\n     */\n    function init(scene) {\n        _scene = scene;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get WiFi wavelength based on channel number.\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel (1-14 for 2.4 GHz, 36-165 for 5 GHz)\n     * @returns {number} Wavelength in meters\n     */\n    function getWavelengthForChannel(channel) {\n        if (!channel || channel < 1) return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n\n        // 2.4 GHz channels: 1-14\n        if (channel <= 14) {\n            return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n        }\n\n        // 5 GHz channels: 36 and above\n        return CONFIG.wavelength_5ghz;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Calculate Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters for a link.\n     * Based on the first Fresnel zone geometry.\n     *\n     * For a link with TX at position P1 and RX at position P2:\n     * - Link distance d = |P1 - P2|\n     * - WiFi wavelength lambda: 5 GHz -> lambda = 0.06m, 2.4 GHz -> lambda = 0.125m\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     * - Ellipsoid centre: midpoint(P1, P2)\n     * - Ellipsoid orientation: major axis along the P1->P2 unit vector\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel) {\n        return calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, 1);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Calculate Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters for a specific zone number.\n     * Based on the nth Fresnel zone geometry.\n     *\n     * For the nth Fresnel zone:\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + n*lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @param {number} zoneNumber - Fresnel zone number (1-based, typically 1-5)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b, zoneNumber }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, zoneNumber) {\n        // Get wavelength based on channel\n        const lambda = getWavelengthForChannel(channel);\n\n        // Direct distance between TX and RX\n        const d = tx.distanceTo(rx);\n\n        // nth Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters\n        // Semi-major axis: a = (d + n*lambda/2) / 2\n        const n = Math.max(1, zoneNumber);\n        const a = (d + n * lambda / 2) / 2;\n\n        // Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n        // Using the property that for a prolate spheroid with foci at tx and rx:\n        // b^2 = a^2 - (d/2)^2\n        const b = Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, a * a - (d / 2) * (d / 2)));\n\n        // Center of ellipsoid (midpoint between TX and RX)\n        const center = new THREE.Vector3().addVectors(tx, rx).multiplyScalar(0.5);\n\n        // Rotation: align with TX-RX axis\n        // X-axis is the major axis of the ellipsoid (a), Y and Z are minor (b)\n        const direction = new THREE.Vector3().subVectors(rx, tx).normalize();\n        const xAxis = new THREE.Vector3(1, 0, 0);\n        const quaternion = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(xAxis, direction);\n\n        return {\n            center: center,\n            semiAxes: new THREE.Vector3(a, b, b), // X (major along link), Y, Z (minor)\n            rotation: quaternion,\n            lambda: lambda,\n            d: d,\n            a: a,\n            b: b,\n            zoneNumber: n,\n            channel: channel\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a Three.js Mesh for a Fresnel zone ellipsoid.\n     * Creates both wireframe and fill meshes for proper visualization.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number\n     * @param {number} color - Color hex value (e.g., 0x4FC3F7 for blue)\n     * @param {Object} options - Optional settings { wireframeOpacity, fillOpacity, zoneNumber }\n     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data } meshes\n     */\n    function FresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options) {\n        if (!_scene) {\n            console.warn('[Fresnel] Scene not initialized. Call Fresnel.init(scene) first.');\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        options = options || {};\n        const wireframeOpacity = options.wireframeOpacity !== undefined ? options.wireframeOpacity : CONFIG.wireframeOpacity;\n        const fillOpacity = options.fillOpacity !== undefined ? options.fillOpacity : CONFIG.fillOpacity;\n        const zoneNumber = options.zoneNumber || 1;\n\n        // Calculate ellipsoid geometry for the specified zone\n        const ellipsoid = calculateFresnelEllipsoidForZone(tx, rx, channel, zoneNumber);\n\n        // Determine segment count based on viewport (mobile optimization)\n        const isMobile = window.innerWidth < CONFIG.mobileViewportWidth;\n        const segments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileSegments : CONFIG.sphereSegments;\n        const heightSegments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileHeightSegments : CONFIG.sphereHeightSegments;\n\n        // Create unit sphere geometry — will be scaled via mesh.scale\n        const geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(1, segments, heightSegments);\n\n        // Create wireframe using EdgesGeometry for crisp edges\n        const edgesGeometry = new THREE.EdgesGeometry(geometry);\n        const wireframeMaterial = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({\n            color: color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: wireframeOpacity,\n            depthTest: true,\n            depthWrite: false\n        });\n        const wireframe = new THREE.LineSegments(edgesGeometry, wireframeMaterial);\n\n        // Create fill mesh\n        const fillMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({\n            color: color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: fillOpacity,\n            depthWrite: false,\n            side: THREE.DoubleSide\n        });\n        const fill = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, fillMaterial);\n\n        // Apply non-uniform scaling: X = semi-major (a), Y = semi-minor (b), Z = semi-minor (b)\n        wireframe.scale.copy(ellipsoid.semiAxes);\n        fill.scale.copy(ellipsoid.semiAxes);\n\n        // Position at ellipsoid center\n        wireframe.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n        fill.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n\n        // Apply rotation to align with link axis\n        wireframe.quaternion.copy(ellipsoid.rotation);\n        fill.quaternion.copy(ellipsoid.rotation);\n\n        // Store metadata for raycasting and interactions\n        const data = {\n            tx: tx.clone(),\n            rx: rx.clone(),\n            channel: channel,\n            zoneNumber: ellipsoid.zoneNumber,\n            lambda: ellipsoid.lambda,\n            d: ellipsoid.d,\n            a: ellipsoid.a,\n            b: ellipsoid.b,\n            semiAxes: ellipsoid.semiAxes.clone(),\n            center: ellipsoid.center.clone(),\n            rotation: ellipsoid.rotation.clone()\n        };\n\n        wireframe.userData = { fresnelEllipsoid: data };\n        fill.userData = { fresnelEllipsoid: data };\n\n        return {\n            wireframe: wireframe,\n            fill: fill,\n            data: data\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a Fresnel ellipsoid to the scene.\n     * Convenience function that creates and adds the mesh.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number\n     * @param {number} color - Color hex value\n     * @param {Object} options - Optional settings\n     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data }\n     */\n    function addFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options) {\n        const ellipsoid = FresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options);\n        if (!ellipsoid) return null;\n\n        if (_scene) {\n            _scene.add(ellipsoid.wireframe);\n            _scene.add(ellipsoid.fill);\n        }\n\n        return ellipsoid;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Remove a Fresnel ellipsoid from the scene.\n     *\n     * @param {Object} ellipsoid - Object returned from addFresnelEllipsoid or FresnelEllipsoid\n     */\n    function removeFresnelEllipsoid(ellipsoid) {\n        if (!ellipsoid) return;\n\n        if (ellipsoid.wireframe) {\n            if (_scene) _scene.remove(ellipsoid.wireframe);\n            if (ellipsoid.wireframe.geometry) ellipsoid.wireframe.geometry.dispose();\n            if (ellipsoid.wireframe.material) ellipsoid.wireframe.material.dispose();\n        }\n\n        if (ellipsoid.fill) {\n            if (_scene) _scene.remove(ellipsoid.fill);\n            if (ellipsoid.fill.geometry) ellipsoid.fill.geometry.dispose();\n            if (ellipsoid.fill.material) ellipsoid.fill.material.dispose();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add multiple Fresnel zone ellipsoids (zones 1-maxZone) for a single link.\n     * Creates wireframe-only ellipsoids for zones 2-5 to avoid visual clutter.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number\n     * @param {number} maxZone - Maximum zone number to create (default 5)\n     * @param {Object} options - Optional settings { zone1Color, zoneColors, wireframeOpacity }\n     * @returns {Array} Array of ellipsoid objects, one per zone\n     */\n    function addFresnelEllipsoidMultiZone(tx, rx, channel, maxZone, options) {\n        if (!_scene) {\n            console.warn('[Fresnel] Scene not initialized.        console.log('[Spaxel] Mobile device: frame rate auto-detection enabled (cap at ' +\n                    (CONFIG.mobileFrameRateCap || 30) + ' FPS if struggling)');\n            }\n        }\n\n controls.screenSpacePanning = true;\n        controls.minDistance = 2;\n        controls.maxDistance = 50;\n        controls.maxPolarAngle = Math.PI / 2 + 0.3; // Allow slight below-ground view\n\n        // Touch-specific optimizations for mobile\n        controls.rotateSpeed = 0.8;           // Rotation speed\n        controls.zoomSpeed = 1.0;             // Zoom speed for pinch gesture (standard speed for accurate touch)\n        controls.panSpeed = 0.8;              // Pan speed for multi-finger drag\n        controls.enablePan = true;            // Enable pan (two-finger or three-finger drag)\n        controls.enableZoom = true;           // Enable zoom (pinch gesture)\n        controls.enableRotate = true;         // Enable rotate (one-finger drag)\n\n        // Touch gesture configuration for OrbitControls\n        // One finger: rotate (orbit)\n        // Two fingers: pinch-to-zoom (dolly) only - NO pan on two fingers\n        // Three fingers: pan (native OrbitControls support)\n        //\n        // Using OrbitControls' built-in touch configuration:\n        // - ONE: THREE.TOUCH.ROTATE (one-finger orbit)\n        // - TWO: THREE.TOUCH.DOLLY (pinch zoom ONLY, no pan)\n        // - THREE: THREE.TOUCH.PAN (three-finger pan)\n        //\n        // Note: THREE.TOUCH.DOLLY (not DOLLY_PAN) ensures two-finger touch\n        // only performs pinch zoom, eliminating accidental pan during zoom.\n        controls.touches = {\n            ONE: THREE.TOUCH.ROTATE,  // One-finger touch rotates the camera\n            TWO: THREE.TOUCH.DOLLY,   // Two-finger touch zooms (pinch) ONLY - no pan\n            THREE: THREE.TOUCH.PAN    // Three-finger touch pans the camera\n        };\n\n        controls.listenToKeyEvents(window); // Enable keyboard controls for desktop\n\n        // Mobile-specific touch handling improvements\n        // Prevent default browser behaviors that interfere with OrbitControls\n        const canvasElement = renderer.domElement;\n\n        // Ensure touch events are properly handled on mobile devices\n        canvasElement.style.touchAction = 'none';\n        canvasElement.style.webkitTouchCallout = 'none';\n        canvasElement.style.webkitUserSelect = 'none';\n        canvasElement.style.userSelect = 'none';\n\n        // Handle iOS Safari-specific touch issues\n        // Prevent double-tap zoom on iOS\n        canvasElement.addEventListener('touchstart', function(event) {\n            if (event.touches.length === 1) {\n                // Store timestamp for double-tap detection\n                canvasElement._lastTouchStart = Date.now();\n            }\n        }, { passive: true });\n\n        canvasElement.addEventListener('touchend', function(event) {\n            if (event.touches.length === 0 && canvasElement._lastTouchStart) {\n                const timeSinceLastTouch = Date.now() - canvasElement._lastTouchStart;\n                // If it's a quick tap (potential double-tap), prevent default\n                if (timeSinceLastTouch < 300) {\n                    event.preventDefault();\n                }\n            }\n        }, { passive: false });\n\n        // Grid helper (XZ plane, Y-up)\n        gridHelper = new THREE.GridHelper(\n            CONFIG.gridWidth,\n            CONFIG.gridDivisions,\n            0x444466,  // center line color\n            0x333344   // grid line color\n        );\n        scene.add(gridHelper);\n\n        // Axes helper for orientation\n        axesHelper = new THREE.AxesHelper(2);\n        axesHelper.position.set(-CONFIG.gridWidth / 2, 0.01, -CONFIG.gridDepth / 2);\n        scene.add(axesHelper);\n\n        // Ambient light\n        const ambientLight = new THREE.AmbientLight(0xffffff, 0.6);\n        scene.add(ambientLight);\n\n        // Directional light\n        const directionalLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff, 0.4);\n        directionalLight.position.set(5, 10, 5);\n        scene.add(directionalLight);\n\n        // Handle window resize\n        window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);\n\n        // Handle orientation change (mobile devices)\n        window.addEventListener('orientationchange', onOrientationChange);\n\n        // Handle visual viewport resize (iOS Safari specific)\n        if (window.visualViewport) {\n            window.visualViewport.addEventListener('resize', function() {\n                // Throttle visual viewport resize events\n                if (orientationChangeTimeout) {\n                    clearTimeout(orientationChangeTimeout);\n                }\n                orientationChangeTimeout = setTimeout(onWindowResize, 50);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Clock for animation mixer delta\n        clock = new THREE.Clock();\n\n        // Initialise 3-D spatial visualisation layer\n        Viz3D.init(scene, camera, controls);\n\n        // Initialise placement (TransformControls, GDOP, room editor)\n        if (window.Placement) {\n            Placement.init(scene, camera, renderer, controls);\n        }\n\n        // Initialise zone editor (TransformControls for zones)\n        if (window.ZoneEditor) {\n            ZoneEditor.init(scene, camera, renderer, controls);\n        }\n\n        // Initialise portal editor (TransformControls for portals)\n        if (window.PortalEditor) {\n            PortalEditor.init(scene, camera, renderer, controls);\n        }\n\n        // Initialize FXAA post-processing on mobile devices\n        // FXAA is used instead of MSAA on mobile for better performance\n        if (window.SpaxelFXAA) {\n            window.SpaxelFXAA.init(scene, camera, renderer).then(function() {\n                console.log('[Spaxel] FXAA initialization complete, active: ' + window.SpaxelFXAA.isActive());\n            }).catch(function(err) {\n                console.error('[Spaxel] FXAA initialization failed:', err);\n            });\n        }\n\n        console.log('[Spaxel] Scene initialized');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get the current viewport dimensions, preferring visualViewport API on iOS Safari.\n     * Falls back to window.innerWidth/Height for browsers that don't support visualViewport.\n     * @returns {Object} {width: number, height: number} Viewport dimensions in pixels\n     */\n    function getViewportDimensions() {\n        // Use visualViewport API on iOS Safari (handles address bar, bottom nav)\n        if (window.visualViewport && window.visualViewport.width > 0) {\n            return {\n                width: window.visualViewport.width,\n                height: window.visualViewport.height\n            };\n        }\n        // Fallback to standard window dimensions\n        return {\n            width: window.innerWidth,\n            height: window.innerHeight\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Handle window resize events with iOS Safari visual viewport support.\n     * Updates renderer size, camera aspect ratio, and projection matrix.\n     */\n    function onWindowResize() {\n        const dims = getViewportDimensions();\n        const width = dims.width;\n        const height = dims.height;\n\n        // Update camera aspect ratio\n        camera.aspect = width / height;\n        camera.updateProjectionMatrix();\n\n        // Update renderer size\n        renderer.setSize(width, height);\n\n        // Update pixel ratio in case it changed (e.g., moving between displays)\n        // Use capped pixel ratio for mobile devices\n        renderer.setPixelRatio(getPixelRatio());\n\n        // Update FXAA resolution if active\n        if (window.SpaxelFXAA && window.SpaxelFXAA.isActive()) {\n            window.SpaxelFXAA.updateResolution();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Handle orientation change events.\n     * Debounced to avoid multiple rapid calls during orientation transition.\n     */\n    var orientationChangeTimeout = null;\n\n    function onOrientationChange() {\n        // Clear any pending resize\n        if (orientationChangeTimeout) {\n            clearTimeout(orientationChangeTimeout);\n        }\n\n        // Debounce resize to allow browser to complete orientation transition\n        // iOS Safari visual viewport may take a moment to stabilize\n        orientationChangeTimeout = setTimeout(function() {\n            // Force a full resize after orientation change completes\n            onWindowResize();\n\n            // Additional visual viewport check for iOS Safari\n            if (window.visualViewport) {\n                // iOS Safari: wait for visual viewport to stabilize\n                // The resize event will fire again once it does\n                window.visualViewport.addEventListener('resize', function onViewportResize() {\n                    onWindowResize();\n                    // Remove listener after first callback\n                    window.visualViewport.removeEventListener('resize', onViewportResize);\n                }, { once: true });\n            }\n        }, 100);\n    }\n\n    function animate() {\n        requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n\n        const now = performance.now();\n        const elapsed = now - state.lastFrameTime;\n\n        // Frame rate capping: skip this frame if not enough time has elapsed\n        if (elapsed < state.minFrameTime) {\n            return; // Skip this frame to maintain target FPS\n        }\n\n        state.lastFrameTime = now;\n\n        controls.update();\n        Viz3D.update();\n        if (window.Placement) Placement.update();\n        // Use FXAA post-processing on mobile, direct rendering on desktop\n        if (window.SpaxelFXAA && window.SpaxelFXAA.isActive()) {\n            window.SpaxelFXAA.render();\n        } else {\n            renderer.render(scene, camera);\n        }\n        updateFPS();\n        detectStrugglingDevice();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Detect struggling devices by monitoring FPS history.\n     * If consistently below threshold FPS on mobile, cap at 30 FPS.\n     * This helps devices that can't maintain 60 FPS by reducing rendering load.\n     */\n    function detectStrugglingDevice() {\n        if (!isMobile() || !CONFIG.autoDetectStrugglingDevice) return;\n\n        // Calculate current FPS based on actual frame rendering time\n        // Use the elapsed time since last frame was RENDERED (after frame skipping)\n        const now = performance.now();\n        const elapsed = now - state.lastFrameTime;\n        const currentFPS = elapsed > 0 ? Math.round(1000 / elapsed) : 60;\n\n        // Maintain FPS history (last 60 samples for more stable detection)\n        state.fpsHistory.push(currentFPS);\n        if (state.fpsHistory.length > 60) {\n            state.fpsHistory.shift();\n        }\n\n        // Only check average FPS after collecting enough samples (1 second at 60fps)\n        if (state.fpsHistory.length >= 60) {\n            const avgFPS = state.fpsHistory.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / state.fpsHistory.length;\n            const minFPS = Math.min(...state.fpsHistory);\n            const maxFPS = Math.max(...state.fpsHistory);\n\n            // Check if device is struggling:\n            // 1. Average FPS is below threshold AND\n            // 2. FPS is consistently low (min and max are both low) AND\n            // 3. We're not already in struggling mode\n            const strugglingThreshold = CONFIG.strugglingDeviceThreshold || 25;\n            const recoveryThreshold = CONFIG.strugglingDeviceRecoveryThreshold || 40;\n\n            if (avgFPS < strugglingThreshold && maxFPS < strugglingThreshold + 10 && !state.strugglingDevice) {\n                // Device is struggling - enable performance mode\n                console.log('[Spaxel] Struggling device detected (avg FPS: ' + avgFPS.toFixed(1) + ', min: ' + minFPS + '), capping at 30 FPS');\n                state.strugglingDevice = true;\n                state.targetFPS = CONFIG.mobileFrameRateCap || 30;\n                state.minFrameTime = 1000 / state.targetFPS;\n\n                // Show a toast notification to inform the user\n                showToast('Performance mode enabled (30 FPS)', 'info');\n\n                // Disable expensive visual effects on struggling devices\n                disableExpensiveEffects();\n            }\n            // Recover if FPS improves consistently\n            else if (avgFPS > recoveryThreshold && minFPS > recoveryThreshold - 5 && state.strugglingDevice) {\n                console.log('[Spaxel] Performance improved (avg FPS: ' + avgFPS.toFixed(1) + '), restoring 60 FPS');\n                state.strugglingDevice = false;\n                state.targetFPS = state.manualFrameRateCap || 60;\n                state.minFrameTime = 1000 / state.targetFPS;\n\n                // Re-enable effects that were disabled\n                enableExpensiveEffects();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Disable expensive visual effects to improve performance on struggling devices.\n     */\n    function disableExpensiveEffects() {\n        // Reduce trail length\n        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.setTrailLength) {\n            window.Viz3D.setTrailLength(20); // Reduce from default\n        }\n\n        // Disable Fresnel zone debug overlay if active\n        if (state.fresnelDebugVisible) {\n            toggleFresnelDebugOverlay(false);\n        }\n\n        // Disable crowd flow visualization\n        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.setFlowLayerVisible) {\n            window.Viz3D.setFlowLayerVisible(false);\n        }\n\n        console.log('[Spaxel] Disabled expensive effects for performance');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Re-enable visual effects when performance recovers.\n     */\n    function enableExpensiveEffects() {\n        // Restore trail length\n        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.setTrailLength) {\n            window.Viz3D.setTrailLength(60); // Restore default\n        }\n\n        console.log('[Spaxel] Re-enabled visual effects');\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // System Quality Gauge\n    // ============================================\n    function updateQualityGauge(score, linkCount, worstLinkID, worstScore) {\n        const valueEl = document.getElementById('quality-value');\n        const fillEl = document.getElementById('quality-gauge-fill');\n        const linkCountEl = document.getElementById('quality-link-count');\n        const worstLinkEl = document.getElementById('quality-worst-link');\n        const worstScoreEl = document.getElementById('quality-worst-score');\n\n        if (!valueEl || !fillEl) return;\n\n        // Update percentage display\n        const pct = Math.round(score * 100);\n        valueEl.textContent = pct + '%';\n\n        // Update circular gauge (stroke-dasharray: circumference = 2 * PI * r = ~81.7 for r=13)\n        const circumference = 2 * Math.PI * 13;\n        const dashLength = (score * circumference).toFixed(1);\n        fillEl.setAttribute('stroke-dasharray', dashLength + ' ' + circumference);\n\n        // Update color based on score\n        let color;\n        if (score >= 0.7) {\n            color = '#66bb6a'; // green\n        } else if (score >= 0.4) {\n            color = '#eab308'; // yellow\n        } else {\n            color = '#ef4444'; // red\n        }\n        fillEl.setAttribute('stroke', color);\n\n        // Update tooltip\n        if (linkCountEl) linkCountEl.textContent = linkCount;\n        if (worstLinkEl) worstLinkEl.textContent = worstLinkID ? abbreviateLinkID(worstLinkID) : '--';\n        if (worstScoreEl) worstScoreEl.textContent = worstScore !== null ? Math.round(worstScore * 100) + '%' : '--';\n    }\n\n    function startHealthPolling() {\n        if (state.healthPollTimer) {\n            clearInterval(state.healthPollTimer);\n        }\n\n        fetchLinkHealth();\n\n        state.healthPollTimer = setInterval(fetchLinkHealth, CONFIG.healthPollIntervalMs);\n    }\n\n    function fetchLinkHealth() {\n        fetch('/api/links')\n            .then(function(res) { return res.json(); })\n            .then(function(links) {\n                handleLinkHealthUpdate(links);\n            })\n            .catch(function(err) {\n                console.error('[Spaxel] Failed to fetch link health:', err);\n            });\n    }\n\n    function handleLinkHealthUpdate(links) {\n        if (!links || links.length === 0) {\n            state.systemHealth = 0;\n            state.worstLinkID = null;\n            state.worstLinkScore = 1.0;\n            updateQualityGauge(0, 0, null, null);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Calculate system health (weighted average of all links)\n        var totalScore = 0;\n        var worstScore = 1.0;\n        var worstID = null;\n\n        // Prepare link data for proactive quality monitoring\n        var linksForProactive = links.map(function(link) {\n            return {\n                link_id: link.link_id,\n                composite_score: link.health_score,\n                quality: link.health_score,\n                health_score: link.health_score,\n                health_details: link.health_details\n            };\n        });\n\n        links.forEach(function(link) {\n            var score = link.health_score !== undefined ? link.health_score : 0.5;\n            totalScore += score;\n\n            if (score < worstScore) {\n                worstScore = score;\n                worstID = link.link_id;\n            }\n        });\n\n        state.systemHealth = totalScore / links.length;\n        state.worstLinkID = worstID;\n        state.worstLinkScore = worstScore;\n\n        updateQualityGauge(state.systemHealth, links.length, worstID, worstScore);\n\n        // Dispatch spaxel:update event for proactive quality monitoring\n        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('spaxel:update', {\n            detail: { links: linksForProactive }\n        }));\n\n        // Also update 3D visualization\n        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.updateLinkHealth) {\n            Viz3D.updateLinkHealth(links);\n        }\n\n        // Also update LinkHealth panel\n        if (window.LinkHealth && window.LinkHealth.updateLinkHealth) {\n            LinkHealth.updateLinkHealth(links);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Diurnal Learning Status\n    // ============================================\n    function startDiurnalPolling() {\n        if (state.diurnalPollTimer) {\n            clearInterval(state.diurnalPollTimer);\n        }\n\n        fetchDiurnalStatus();\n\n        state.diurnalPollTimer = setInterval(fetchDiurnalStatus, CONFIG.diurnalPollIntervalMs);\n    }\n\n    function fetchDiurnalStatus() {\n        fetch('/api/diurnal/status')\n            .then(function(res) { return res.json(); })\n            .then(function(statuses) {\n                handleDiurnalStatusUpdate(statuses);\n            })\n            .catch(function(err) {\n                console.error('[Spaxel] Failed to fetch diurnal status:', err);\n            });\n    }\n\n    function handleDiurnalStatusUpdate(statuses) {\n        if (!statuses || statuses.length === 0) {\n            updateDiurnalBanner(null);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Find the link with the longest remaining learning time\n        var worstStatus = null;\n        statuses.forEach(function(status) {\n            state.diurnalStatus.set(status.link_id, status);\n            if (!worstStatus || status.days_remaining > worstStatus.days_remaining) {\n                if (status.is_learning) {\n                    worstStatus = status;\n                }\n            }\n        });\n\n        updateDiurnalBanner(worstStatus);\n    }\n\n    function updateDiurnalBanner(status) {\n        var banner = document.getElementById('diurnal-banner');\n        var message = document.getElementById('diurnal-message');\n        var progress = document.getElementById('diurnal-progress');\n        var daysLeft = document.getElementById('diurnal-days-left');\n\n        if (!banner) return;\n\n        if (!status || !status.is_learning) {\n            banner.classList.remove('visible');\n            return;\n        }\n\n        banner.classList.add('visible');\n\n        if (message) {\n            message.textContent = 'Learning your home\\'s daily patterns...';\n        }\n\n        if (progress) {\n            var pct = Math.min(100, Math.max(0, status.progress || 0));\n            progress.style.width = pct + '%';\n        }\n\n        if (daysLeft) {\n            var days = Math.ceil(status.days_remaining || 0);\n            if (days > 0) {\n                daysLeft.textContent = days + (days === 1 ? ' day left' : ' days left');\n            } else {\n                daysLeft.textContent = 'Almost ready...';\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    function showToast(message, type) {\n        var container = document.getElementById('toast-container');\n        if (!container) return;\n\n        var toast = document.createElement('div');\n        toast.className = 'toast toast-' + (type || 'info');\n        toast.textContent = message;\n\n        container.appendChild(toast);\n\n        setTimeout(function() {\n            toast.classList.add('fade-out');\n            setTimeout(function() {\n                if (toast.parentNode) {\n                    toast.parentNode.removeChild(toast);\n                }\n            }, 300);\n        }, 5000);\n    }\n\n    function updateFPS() {\n        state.frameCount++;\n        const now = performance.now();\n        const elapsed = now - state.lastFpsTime;\n        if (elapsed >= 1000) {\n            const fps = Math.round(state.frameCount * 1000 / elapsed);\n            document.getElementById('fps-counter').textContent = fps;\n            state.frameCount = 0;\n            state.lastFpsTime = now;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // WebSocket Connection (via SpaxelWebSocket)\n    // ============================================\n    function connectWebSocket() {\n        // Initialize the WebSocket manager with callbacks\n        SpaxelWebSocket.init({\n            onOpen: function(ws) {\n                console.log('[Spaxel] WebSocket connected');\n                state.wsConnected = true;\n                state.awaitingSnapshot = true;\n            },\n            onMessage: function(data) {\n                handleMessage(data);\n            },\n            onClose: function(event) {\n                console.log('[Spaxel] WebSocket closed:', event.code, event.reason);\n                state.wsConnected = false;\n\n                // Start blob extrapolation using captured blob states\n                SpaxelWebSocket.startExtrapolation();\n            },\n            onError: function(error) {\n                console.error('[Spaxel] WebSocket error:', error);\n            }\n        });\n\n        SpaxelWebSocket.connect();\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Message Handling\n    // ============================================\n\n    // Event handlers for new message types\n\n    function handleEventMessage(msg) {\n        if (!msg.event) return;\n\n        const event = msg.event;\n\n        // Dedup: skip if we already processed this event (from immediate broadcast or prior delta)\n        const eid = String(event.id);\n        if (state.recentEventIDs.has(eid)) return;\n        state.recentEventIDs.add(eid);\n\n        // Prune old IDs every 30 seconds to prevent unbounded growth\n        const now = Date.now();\n        if (now > state.recentEventIDsPruneAt) {\n            state.recentEventIDs.clear();\n            state.recentEventIDsPruneAt = now + 30000;\n        }\n\n        console.log('[Spaxel] Event:', event.kind, 'in', event.zone, 'by', event.person_name || 'blob #' + event.blob_id);\n\n        // Log to timeline\n        const timeStr = new Date(event.ts).toLocaleTimeString();\n        let description = '';\n\n        if (event.kind === 'zone_entry') {\n            description = (event.person_name || 'Someone') + ' entered ' + event.zone;\n        } else if (event.kind === 'zone_exit') {\n            description = (event.person_name || 'Someone') + ' left ' + event.zone;\n        } else if (event.kind === 'portal_crossing') {\n            description = (event.person_name || 'Someone') + ' crossed portal in ' + event.zone;\n        } else if (event.kind === 'presence_transition') {\n            description = (event.person_name || 'Someone') + ' presence detected in ' + event.zone;\n        } else {\n            description = event.kind + ' in ' + event.zone;\n        }\n\n        logTimelineEvent(event.kind, null, description + ' (' + timeStr + ')');\n\n        // Show toast for security-relevant events\n        if (event.kind === 'zone_entry' || event.kind === 'portal_crossing') {\n            showToast(description, 'info');\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleAlertMessage(msg) {\n        if (!msg.alert) return;\n\n        const alert = msg.alert;\n        console.log('[Spaxel] Alert:', alert.severity, alert.description);\n\n        // Show toast notification\n        const toastType = alert.severity === 'critical' ? 'error' : 'warning';\n        showToast(alert.description, toastType);\n\n        // Log to timeline\n        const timeStr = new Date(alert.ts).toLocaleTimeString();\n        logTimelineEvent('alert', null, '[' + alert.severity.toUpperCase() + '] ' + alert.description + ' (' + timeStr + ')');\n\n        // Could trigger UI alert state here (e.g., show alert banner)\n        if (window.showAlertBanner) {\n            window.showAlertBanner(alert);\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleBLEScanMessage(msg) {\n        if (!msg.devices || !Array.isArray(msg.devices)) return;\n\n        console.log('[Spaxel] BLE scan: ' + msg.devices.length + ' devices');\n\n        // Update BLE device list state\n        if (!state.bleDevices) {\n            state.bleDevices = new Map();\n        }\n\n        // Clear previous entries and add current devices\n        state.bleDevices.clear();\n        msg.devices.forEach(function (device) {\n            state.bleDevices.set(device.mac || device.addr, {\n                mac: device.mac || device.addr,\n                name: device.name || device.device_name || 'Unknown',\n                rssi: device.rssi || device.rssi_dbm || 0,\n                last_seen: device.last_seen || Date.now(),\n                label: device.label || '',\n                blob_id: device.blob_id || null\n            });\n        });\n\n        // Update UI if BLE panel exists\n        if (window.BLEPanel && window.BLEPanel.updateDevices) {\n            window.BLEPanel.updateDevices(msg.devices);\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleTriggerStateMessage(msg) {\n        if (!msg.trigger) return;\n\n        const trigger = msg.trigger;\n        console.log('[Spaxel] Trigger state:', trigger.name, 'enabled=' + trigger.enabled);\n\n        // Update trigger state in UI if automation panel exists\n        if (window.Automations && window.Automations.updateTriggerState) {\n            window.Automations.updateTriggerState(trigger);\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleSystemHealthMessage(msg) {\n        if (!msg.health) return;\n\n        const health = msg.health;\n\n        // Update system health display in UI\n        const healthEl = document.getElementById('system-uptime');\n        if (healthEl) {\n            const uptimeSec = health.uptime_s || 0;\n            const days = Math.floor(uptimeSec / 86400);\n            const hours = Math.floor((uptimeSec % 86400) / 3600);\n            const mins = Math.floor((uptimeSec % 3600) / 60);\n            if (days > 0) {\n                healthEl.textContent = days + 'd ' + hours + 'h ' + mins + 'm';\n            } else {\n                healthEl.textContent = hours + 'h ' + mins + 'm';\n            }\n        }\n\n        const memEl = document.getElementById('system-memory');\n        if (memEl) {\n            memEl.textContent = (health.mem_mb || 0).toFixed(1) + ' MB';\n        }\n\n        const goroutinesEl = document.getElementById('system-goroutines');\n        if (goroutinesEl) {\n            goroutinesEl.textContent = health.go_routines || 0;\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleMessage(data) {\n        if (typeof data === 'string') {\n            // JSON message\n            try {\n                const msg = JSON.parse(data);\n                handleJSONMessage(msg);\n            } catch (e) {\n                console.error('[Spaxel] Failed to parse JSON:', e);\n            }\n        } else if (data instanceof ArrayBuffer) {\n            // Binary CSI frame\n            handleBinaryFrame(data);\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleJSONMessage(msg) {\n        // Snapshot: first message on every connect/reconnect.  Contains full state.\n        if (msg.type === 'snapshot') {\n            handleSnapshot(msg);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Incremental update: 10 Hz delta with no type field.\n        // Only fields that changed since last tick are present.\n        if (!msg.type) {\n            handleIncrementalUpdate(msg);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        switch (msg.type) {\n            case 'state':\n                // Initial state dump\n                if (msg.nodes) {\n                    msg.nodes.forEach(node => {\n                        state.nodes.set(node.mac, {\n                            mac: node.mac,\n                            firmware: node.firmware_version,\n                            chip: node.chip,\n                            lastSeen: Date.now()\n                        });\n                    });\n                }\n                if (msg.links) {\n                    msg.links.forEach(link => {\n                        const existing = state.links.get(link.id) || {};\n                        state.links.set(link.id, {\n                            nodeMAC: link.node_mac,\n                            peerMAC: link.peer_mac,\n                            lastFrame: Date.now(),\n                            lastCSI: existing.lastCSI || null,\n                            motionDetected: existing.motionDetected || false,\n                            deltaRMS: existing.deltaRMS || 0,\n                            ampHistory: existing.ampHistory || [],\n                            lastAmpSample: existing.lastAmpSample || 0\n                        });\n                    });\n                }\n                if (msg.motion_states) {\n                    msg.motion_states.forEach(ms => applyMotionState(ms));\n                }\n                updateNodeList();\n                updateLinkList();\n                Viz3D.applyLinks(msg.links || []);\n                break;\n\n            case 'node_connected':\n                state.nodes.set(msg.mac, {\n                    mac: msg.mac,\n                    firmware: msg.firmware_version,\n                    chip: msg.chip,\n                    unpaired: !!msg.unpaired,\n                    lastSeen: Date.now()\n                });\n                updateNodeList();\n                if (window.SpaxelTroubleshoot) {\n                    window.SpaxelTroubleshoot.handleEvent('node_connected', msg);\n                }\n                // Show first-time tooltips on first node connection\n                if (window.SpaxelTooltips && state.nodes.size === 1) {\n                    setTimeout(function () { window.SpaxelTooltips.showSequence(); }, 2000);\n                }\n                break;\n\n            case
